***verbetering.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verbetering.html>verbetering</a> (9624)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">verbeteringe</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verbeteren.html>verbeteren</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verbetering.html>verbetering</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verbetering.html>verbeteringen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verbetering.html>verbeteringetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>An improvement, amelioration</li>
<li>A correction, rectification,</li>
<li>A reparation, amendment</li>
<li>The act or process of improving, correcting etc.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A reprimand; correction, sanction</li>
<li>A raise, promotion etc.</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verbloemen.html>verbloemen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of a plant</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to blossom again, bear (at least) a second bloom</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to ornate, to cover with flowers</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to <a href = vnd.unilang:veilen.html>veil</a>, soften by euphemistic phrasing</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to excuse, treat apologetically</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to mask, hide (something unpleasant)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to avoid, suppress, leave unspoken</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to personify</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chemistry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to effloresce, let crystallize</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verbranden.html>verbranden</a> (3274)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:branden.html>branden</a></i>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verbranden.html>verbranden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To burn, consume/kill in fire</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To be consumed by fire</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To burn, affect gravely with corrosive etc. chemicals</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To burn, be affected gravely with corrosive etc. chemicals</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To discredit completely, ruin psychologically for future use, e.g. by scandal or media leak
